<li><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>'s economy grows at 9% in the latest period, on course to become the largest economy in the world by 2050.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup></li>
<li>A 197 ft (<span class="nowrap">60 m</span>) spire is inserted on <a href="/wiki/Taipei_101" title="Taipei 101">Taipei 101</a> in <a href="/wiki/Taipei" title="Taipei">Taipei</a>, Taiwan, unseating Malaysia's <a href="/wiki/Petronas_Towers" title="Petronas Towers">Petronas Towers</a> as the world's tallest building.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_18.2C_2003_.28Saturday.29">October 18, 2003 (Saturday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: October 18, 2003 (Saturday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Leaders of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific-rim_nations" title="Pacific-rim nations">Pacific-rim nations</a> gather in <a href="/wiki/Bangkok" title="Bangkok">Bangkok</a> ahead of the 11th <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_Pacific_Economic_Cooperation" title="Asian Pacific Economic Cooperation">Asian Pacific Economic Cooperation</a> (APEC) conference.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/President" title="President">President</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> arrives in <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> ahead of an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/APEC" title="APEC">APEC</a> summit of 21 <a href="/wiki/Asia-Pacific" title="Asia-Pacific">Asia-Pacific</a> <a href="/wiki/Forms_of_government" title="Forms of government">government</a> leaders which is likely to be dominated by discussions of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_on_Terrorism" title="War on Terrorism">War on Terrorism</a> and <a href="/wiki/Trade" title="Trade">trade</a> friction between <a href="/wiki/Wealth" title="Wealth">rich</a> and <a href="/wiki/Poverty" title="Poverty">poor</a> <a href="/wiki/Nation" title="Nation">nations</a> (trade and currency).</li>
<li>New audio tapes, allegedly from <a href="/wiki/Osama_bin_Laden" title="Osama bin Laden">Osama bin Laden</a>, air on the <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> network.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">occupation of Iraq</a>: <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>'s government, one of the staunchest supporters of the attack on Iraq, has pledged <span class="nowrap">$300 million</span> over several years toward Iraqi reconstruction.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>'s state oil corporation is reported to have run out of fuel, aggravating the continuing acute fuel crisis.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup></li>
<li>Officials declare a state of emergency due to severe <a href="/wiki/Flood" title="Flood">flooding</a> in <a href="/wiki/Squamish,_British_Columbia" title="Squamish, British Columbia">Squamish</a>, British Columbia. Parts of the town are evacuated.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup></li>
<li>Canadian <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Jean_Chr%C3%A9tien" title="Jean Chrétien">Jean Chrétien</a>, visiting <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>'s President <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Karzai" title="Hamid Karzai">Hamid Karzai</a>, is whisked out of <a href="/wiki/Kabul" title="Kabul">Kabul</a> owing to reports of a rocket attack. The reports turn out to be unfounded.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_19.2C_2003_.28Sunday.29">October 19, 2003 (Sunday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: October 19, 2003 (Sunday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>A new biography, reported in <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Times_(UK)" title="The Sunday Times (UK)">The Sunday Times</a></i>, claims that the prosecution of <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Wilde" title="Oscar Wilde">Oscar Wilde</a> for <a href="/wiki/Sodomy" title="Sodomy">sodomy</a> was ordered by the then <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_(UK)" title="Liberal Party (UK)">Liberal</a> government, in a deal with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/John_Sholto_Douglas,_9th_Marquess_of_Queensberry" title="John Sholto Douglas, 9th Marquess of Queensberry">Marquess of Queensberry</a>, the father of <a href="/wiki/Lord_Alfred_Douglas" title="Lord Alfred Douglas">Lord Alfred Douglas</a>, to prevent his exposure of a homosexual relationship between another of his sons, Viscount Drumlanrig, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Prime_Minister" title="British Prime Minister">British Prime Minister</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Archibald_Philip_Primrose,_5th_Earl_of_Rosebery" title="Archibald Philip Primrose, 5th Earl of Rosebery">Lord Rosebery</a>. According to reports, future prime minister <a href="/wiki/H._H._Asquith" title="H. H. Asquith">H. H. Asquith</a> played a key role in negotiating the deal, which led to the imprisonment of the Irish writer.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Prime_Minister" title="British Prime Minister">British Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Tony_Blair" title="Tony Blair">Tony Blair</a> is rushed to hospital with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heart_disease" title="Heart disease">heart problems</a>. An <a href="/wiki/Cardiac_arrhythmia" title="Cardiac arrhythmia">irregular heart-beat</a> is diagnosed. Blair is given a <a href="/wiki/Cardioversion" title="Cardioversion">cardioversion</a> in hospital, where he stays for four or five hours before going back to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Number_10_Downing_Street" title="Number 10 Downing Street">Number 10 Downing Street</a>, and is ordered by his doctors to take 24 hours complete rest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118"><a href="#cite_note-118">[118]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pope_John_Paul_II" title="Pope John Paul II">Pope John Paul II</a> beatifies <a href="/wiki/Mother_Teresa" title="Mother Teresa">Mother Teresa</a>. Hundreds of thousands attend the ceremony in <a href="/wiki/St._Peter%27s_Square" title="St. Peter's Square">St. Peter's Square</a>. Mother Teresa, who founded the <a href="/wiki/Missionaries_of_Charity" title="Missionaries of Charity">Missionaries of Charity</a>, is now one step from sainthood.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119"><a href="#cite_note-119">[119]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> and the United States are reported to be discussing the possible withdrawal of thousands of US troops.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120"><a href="#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Korea_nuclear_weapons_program" title="North Korea nuclear weapons program">North Korea crisis</a>: The United States says it is willing to give <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> security assurances in exchange for a <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_warfare" title="Nuclear warfare">nuclear</a> standdown. U.S. <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">President Bush</a> rules out a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Non-aggression_treaty" title="Non-aggression treaty">non-aggression treaty</a> demanded by <a href="/wiki/Pyongyang" title="Pyongyang">Pyongyang</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-121"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bomb" title="Bomb">Bomb</a> blows up a <a href="/wiki/Pickup_truck" title="Pickup truck">pickup truck</a> on a dirt road in Afghanistan's eastern <a href="/wiki/Kunar_Province" title="Kunar Province">Kunar Province</a>, killing four people, and two Afghan soldiers are killed in a separate <a href="/wiki/Land_mine" title="Land mine">land mine</a> explosion in the country's south. The explosions come two days after the <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> <i>allegedly</i> distributed pamphlets warning against working with the post-<a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> government of President <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Karzai" title="Hamid Karzai">Hamid Karzai</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli-Palestinian_conflict" title="Israeli-Palestinian conflict">Israeli-Palestinian conflict</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> gunmen attack an <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> army foot patrol near a <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a> village, kills three soldiers and wounds a fourth, rescue services and security sources state. Gunfire attacks near the Palestinian village of <a href="/wiki/Ein_Yabrud" title="Ein Yabrud">Ein Yabrud</a>, east of the town of <a href="/wiki/Ramallah" title="Ramallah">Ramallah</a>, not far from the <a href="/wiki/Israeli_settlement" title="Israeli settlement">Israeli settlement</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ofra" title="Ofra">Ofra</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: A <a href="/wiki/Fallujah" title="Fallujah">Fallujah</a> roadside attack on a military <a href="/wiki/Convoy" title="Convoy">convoy</a> leaves an American <a href="/wiki/Armored_car_(military)" title="Armored car (military)">armored car</a> and <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Munitions_truck&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Munitions truck (page does not exist)">munitions truck</a> burning wrecks. No one was reported killed. <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqis</a> nearby were reportedly cheering. Emerging series of threats.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124"><a href="#cite_note-124">[124]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_20.2C_2003_.28Monday.29">October 20, 2003 (Monday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: October 20, 2003 (Monday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Canadian <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Jean_Chr%C3%A9tien" title="Jean Chrétien">Jean Chrétien</a> indicates that during an informal meeting between him and <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a>, the Russian president indicated that he was tentatively in favour of signing the <a href="/wiki/Kyoto_Protocol" title="Kyoto Protocol">Kyoto Protocol</a>. Russia's signature is absolutely necessary for the protocol to acquire the force of law.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125"><a href="#cite_note-125">[125]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_deficit" title="United States deficit">United States deficit</a>: The United States posts a record budget deficit of <span class="nowrap">$374.2 billion</span> in the <a href="/wiki/Fiscal_year" title="Fiscal year">fiscal year</a> ending September 30. The figure broke the previous record of <span class="nowrap">$290 billion</span>, set in 1992. The number was actually better than the U.S. government's own forecast of <span class="nowrap">$455 billion</span>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126"><a href="#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup></li>
<li>United States: The publicist of <a href="/wiki/Robert_De_Niro" title="Robert De Niro">Robert De Niro</a> announces that the actor has prostate cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup></li>
<li>Early results in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Swiss_elections,_2003" title="Swiss elections, 2003">Swiss elections</a> show larger-than-predicted gains for the right-wing <a href="/wiki/Swiss_People%27s_Party" title="Swiss People's Party">Swiss People's Party</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup></li>
<li>An Italian archaeologist claims to have found a carved two-faced head over 200,000 years old. The carving is possible the work of <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_erectus" title="Homo erectus">Homo erectus</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup></li>
<li>[The <a href="/wiki/Soyuz_TMA-3" title="Soyuz TMA-3">Soyuz TMA-3</a> spacecraft docked with the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a> bringing a new crew of three from Russia, the United States, and <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130"><a href="#cite_note-130">[130]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_21.2C_2003_.28Tuesday.29">October 21, 2003 (Tuesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: October 21, 2003 (Tuesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_on_Terrorism" title="War on Terrorism">War on Terrorism</a>: US officials state that they believe <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wall_Street_Journal" title="Wall Street Journal">Wall Street Journal</a></i> reporter <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Pearl" title="Daniel Pearl">Daniel Pearl</a> was killed by <a href="/wiki/Khalid_Sheikh_Mohammed" title="Khalid Sheikh Mohammed">Khalid Sheikh Mohammed</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup></li>
<li>Scientists call for a total ban on fishing for <a href="/wiki/Cod" title="Cod">cod</a> in the <a href="/wiki/North_Sea" title="North Sea">North Sea</a> to allow stocks to recover from near extinction.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup></li>
<li>The commander of <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> forces in Afghanistan warns that the security of <a href="/wiki/Kabul" title="Kabul">Kabul</a> is at risk if security is not achieved in the Afghan countryside.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> (HRW) accuses US troops of using excessive force against civilians in Iraq.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>'s Supreme Council agrees to comply with the <a href="/wiki/International_Atomic_Energy_Agency" title="International Atomic Energy Agency">International Atomic Energy Agency</a>, allow inspections of its nuclear facilities, and suspend its <a href="/wiki/Uranium" title="Uranium">uranium</a> enrichment program.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup></li>
<li>Outbreaks of <a href="/wiki/Locust" title="Locust">locusts</a> are reported in <a href="/wiki/Mauritania" title="Mauritania">Mauritania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Niger" title="Niger">Niger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> and might spread to other areas of <a href="/wiki/North_Africa" title="North Africa">north Africa</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup></li>
<li>In a series of moves designed to bring about final implementation of the <a href="/wiki/Good_Friday_Agreement" title="Good Friday Agreement">Good Friday Agreement</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Government" title="British Government">British Government</a> confirms that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Elections" title="Elections">elections</a> to the region's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Devolved_administration" title="Devolved administration">devolved administration</a> will be held on November 26. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Provisional_IRA" title="Provisional IRA">Provisional IRA</a> announces a further act of weapons decommissioning. <a href="/wiki/Sinn_F%C3%A9in" title="Sinn Féin">Sinn Féin</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Gerry_Adams" title="Gerry Adams">Gerry Adams</a> declares "the end to physical force republicanism". Statements from all the major parties involved are expected over the course of the day.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140"><a href="#cite_note-140">[140]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli-Palestinian_conflict" title="Israeli-Palestinian conflict">Israeli-Palestinian conflict</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UN_General_Assembly" title="UN General Assembly">UN General Assembly</a> approves a resolution demanding that <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> remove a security fence in the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>. The resolution passes by an overwhelming majority of 144 to 4 with the US voting against the motion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_and_Labrador_general_election,_2003" title="Newfoundland and Labrador general election, 2003">Newfoundland and Labrador general election, 2003</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Progressive_Conservative_Party_of_Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Progressive Conservative Party of Newfoundland and Labrador">Tories</a> of <a href="/wiki/Danny_Williams_(politician)" title="Danny Williams (politician)">Danny Williams</a> defeat the incumbent <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Liberal Party of Newfoundland and Labrador">Liberals</a> under <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Newfoundland_and_Labrador_Premiers" title="List of Newfoundland and Labrador Premiers">Premier</a> <a href="/wiki/Roger_Grimes" title="Roger Grimes">Roger Grimes</a>, taking more than two-thirds of the seats in the House of Assembly.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a> – A trial opens in Lago Agrio in which US oil company ChevronTexaco is charged with polluting a once-pristine swath of the Amazon rainforest. The plaintiffs' lawyers have put a <span class="nowrap">US$1 billion</span> price tag on clean up and medical care for the region's inhabitants.</li>
</ul>
<p><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_22.2C_2003_.28Wednesday.29">October 22, 2003 (Wednesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: October 22, 2003 (Wednesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>India launches a peace initiative to normalise relations with <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. Formal talks are conditional on <a href="/wiki/Islamabad" title="Islamabad">Islamabad</a> ending <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmiri</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cross-border_terrorism" title="Cross-border terrorism">cross-border terrorism</a> initiatives.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mahathir_bin_Mohamad" title="Mahathir bin Mohamad">Mahathir bin Mohamad</a>, outgoing <a href="/wiki/Prime_minister" title="Prime minister">prime minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, accuses leading democratic nations of terrorising the world. He seemed to be referring to the US, <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>, and Australia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: The commander of US ground forces in <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> says that <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">Al-Qaeda</a> is now operating in Iraq as witnessed by increasingly sophisticated attacks on US troops.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_detainment_camp" title="Guantanamo Bay detainment camp">Guantanamo Bay</a>: Leaders of the European Union parliament urge the EU to take action over 26 Europeans being held indefinitely by the US without charges, without trial, without legal representation at Guantanamo Bay. The detainees are experiencing increasing psychological problems.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> (HRW) releases a report about <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mental_illness" title="Mental illness">mentally ill</a> inmates of United States <a href="/wiki/Prison" title="Prison">prisons</a>. It concludes that mentally ill offenders are frequently physically abused, punished by staff for self-destructive behavior and not given the treatment they need.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup></li>
<li>Top British runner <a href="/wiki/Dwain_Chambers" title="Dwain Chambers">Dwain Chambers</a> tests positive for the drug <a href="/wiki/Tetrahydrogestrinone" title="Tetrahydrogestrinone">tetrahydrogestrinone</a> (THG). The <a href="/wiki/Steroid" title="Steroid">steroid</a> was previously believed to be undetectable but an anonymous source provided a used syringe containing traces last week.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_23.2C_2003_.28Thursday.29">October 23, 2003 (Thursday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: October 23, 2003 (Thursday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Luis_A._Ferr%C3%A9" title="Luis A. Ferré">Luis A. Ferré</a>, the third Democratically Elected <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Governor of Puerto Rico">Governor of Puerto Rico</a>, dies at age 99.</li>
<li>Canada: <a href="/wiki/Dalton_McGuinty" title="Dalton McGuinty">Dalton McGuinty</a> is sworn in as the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Ontario_premiers" title="List of Ontario premiers">24th premier</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ontario" title="Ontario">Ontario</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: There is every sign that the international conference in Madrid at which pledges to re-build Iraq are hoped for will disappoint and e.g. <a href="/wiki/Paul_Bremer" title="Paul Bremer">Paul Bremer</a> seeks to lower expectations.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">United States Supreme Court</a>: Before a conservative legal organization, Supreme Court Justice <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Scalia" title="Antonin Scalia">Antonin Scalia</a> ridicules the recent Supreme Court decision overturning anti-sodomy laws in <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, saying that the Court had "held to be a constitutional right what had been a criminal offense at the time of the founding and for nearly 200 years thereafter." According to news reports, Scalia adopted a mocking tone to read from the court's ruling.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=AL_Arabi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="AL Arabi (page does not exist)">Kuwait</a> AL Arabi football club beat Qadsia in the Kuwait derby 2–0.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_24.2C_2003_.28Friday.29">October 24, 2003 (Friday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: October 24, 2003 (Friday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>49 <a href="/wiki/Miner" title="Miner">miners</a> are trapped in a Russian mine as water began seeping into the mine, disabling electrical systems.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli-Palestinian_conflict" title="Israeli-Palestinian conflict">Israeli-Palestinian conflict</a>: The body of the Hamas militant killed in the attack on an Israeli military camp (that killed three Israeli soldiers) is returned to his family in their refugee camp.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2003_invasion_of_Iraq" title="2003 invasion of Iraq">2003 invasion of Iraq</a>: The US Senate Committee on Intelligence finalizes its report on pre-war intelligence and is highly critical of <a href="/wiki/George_Tenet" title="George Tenet">George Tenet</a> and the quality of US intelligence about Iraq's weapons.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup></li>
<li>Earth is hit by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Halloween_Solar_Storm" title="Halloween Solar Storm">Halloween Solar Storm</a>, disrupting some <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Satellite_communications" title="Satellite communications">satellite communications</a> but not <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Electric_power_transmission_grid" title="Electric power transmission grid">electric power transmission grids</a> as was predicted. Canada, the northern US northern Europe were treated to an exceptional display of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aurora_borealis" title="Aurora borealis">aurora borealis</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup></li>
<li>The final flights of <a href="/wiki/Concorde" title="Concorde">Concorde</a>, from New York, Edinburgh, and a loop around the Bay of Biscay, touch down at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heathrow_International_Airport" title="Heathrow International Airport">Heathrow International Airport</a> around 1600 BST, marking the end of 27 years of commercial supersonic flight.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup></li>
<li>Three same-sex couples in <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>, including a <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a> city councilman, apply for marriage licenses. They state that if the registry judge does not grant them the licenses, they will appeal to Spain's constitutional court, and as far as the <a href="/wiki/European_Court_of_Human_Rights" title="European Court of Human Rights">European Court of Human Rights</a> if necessary. They describe their actions as inspired by <a href="/wiki/Same-sex_marriage_in_Canada" title="Same-sex marriage in Canada">the recent rulings on same-sex marriage</a> in Canada.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_25.2C_2003_.28Saturday.29">October 25, 2003 (Saturday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: October 25, 2003 (Saturday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The Indian philosopher and Hindu revivalist <a href="/wiki/Pandurang_Shastri_Athavale" title="Pandurang Shastri Athavale">Pandurang Shastri Athavale</a> dies at the age of 83.</li>
<li>Israel publishes map of fence.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/World_Series" title="World Series">World Series</a>: <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">Baseball</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Florida_Marlins" title="Florida Marlins">Florida Marlins</a> defeat the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Yankees" title="New York Yankees">New York Yankees</a>, four games to two, to win the <a href="/wiki/2003_World_Series" title="2003 World Series">2003 World Series</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: A US <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UH-60_Black_Hawk" title="UH-60 Black Hawk">Blackhawk</a> helicopter is brought down near <a href="/wiki/Tikrit" title="Tikrit">Tikrit</a> by <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> militants. The Daily Star Lebanon reports that the US is effectively plundering Iraq following the occupation.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup> The daily average of attacks on US troops rises and reaches about 25–26 per day.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup> 100,000 march against the occupation of Iraq in Washington DC.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup></li>
<li>Tony Blair announces that the UK will press ahead with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GM_technology" title="GM technology">GM technology</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup></li>
<li>Many countries in the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Hemisphere" title="Northern Hemisphere">Northern Hemisphere</a> will end <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time" title="Daylight saving time">daylight saving time</a> in the night from October 25 to October 26. In the <a href="/wiki/Southern_Hemisphere" title="Southern Hemisphere">Southern Hemisphere</a> daylight saving time will start only in the Australian states of <a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales" title="New South Wales">New South Wales</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Australia" title="South Australia">South Australia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Victoria_(Australia)" title="Victoria (Australia)">Victoria</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_26.2C_2003_.28Sunday.29">October 26, 2003 (Sunday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: October 26, 2003 (Sunday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wildfire" title="Wildfire">Wildfires</a> start to rage in <a href="/wiki/Southern_California" title="Southern California">Southern California</a>. The scheduled <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NFL" title="NFL">NFL</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Monday_Night_Football" title="Monday Night Football">Monday Night Football</a></i> game between the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Diego_Chargers" title="San Diego Chargers">San Diego Chargers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Miami_Dolphins" title="Miami Dolphins">Miami Dolphins</a> is relocated from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Diego,_California" title="San Diego, California">San Diego</a>, California, to <a href="/wiki/Tempe,_Arizona" title="Tempe, Arizona">Tempe</a>, Arizona, as a consequence of the fires.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Rashid_Hotel" title="Al-Rashid Hotel">Al-Rashid Hotel</a> in <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a> where US deputy defense secretary <a href="/wiki/Paul_Wolfowitz" title="Paul Wolfowitz">Paul Wolfowitz</a> was staying has been evacuated after several rockets were fired at it in the morning. one US Colonel was killed and fifteen individuals wounded (three seriously) in the attack.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172"><a href="#cite_note-172">[172]</a></sup> Two more explosions occurred near Al Rashid hotel later towards the evening. Further investigations confirm that Iraq had no active nuclear program, but did not relinquish nuclear ambitions or technical records.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174"><a href="#cite_note-174">[174]</a></sup></li>
<li>The President of Syria says that Iran and Syria, which are increasingly close allies, are capable of neutralizing conspiracies of foreign powers (implicitly referring to the US and Israel).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175"><a href="#cite_note-175">[175]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Khodorkovsky" title="Mikhail Khodorkovsky">Mikhail Khodorkovsky</a>, Russia's wealthiest businessman, has been arrested and is being held in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> facing charges of fraud and tax evasion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176"><a href="#cite_note-176">[176]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_27.2C_2003_.28Monday.29">October 27, 2003 (Monday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: October 27, 2003 (Monday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: More than 40 people are killed and over 200 are injured in a wave of coordinated bomb attacks on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Red_Cross" title="Red Cross">Red Cross</a> compound and several local police stations in <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177"><a href="#cite_note-177">[177]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> states that the bombings are a sign of desperation by the insurgents.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178"><a href="#cite_note-178">[178]</a></sup></li>
<li>U.S. fund group <a href="/wiki/Putnam_Investments" title="Putnam Investments">Putnam Investments</a> fires four fund managers as scandals about improper and/or fraudulent dealings reach the mutual fund industry.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179"><a href="#cite_note-179">[179]</a></sup></li>
<li>Former Japanese Prime Ministers <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Miyazawa_Kiichi" title="Miyazawa Kiichi">Miyazawa Kiichi</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nakasone_Yasuhiro" title="Nakasone Yasuhiro">Nakasone Yasuhiro</a> announce that they are going to retire.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Northwest_Territories_general_election,_2003" title="Northwest Territories general election, 2003">Northwest Territories general election, 2003</a>: The writ is dropped for the 19 electoral districts of the <a href="/wiki/Northwest_Territories" title="Northwest Territories">Northwest Territories</a> to elect members to the 15th session of the <a href="/wiki/Consensus_government" title="Consensus government">consensus government</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_28.2C_2003_.28Tuesday.29">October 28, 2003 (Tuesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: October 28, 2003 (Tuesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The United States <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Reserve" title="Federal Reserve">Federal Reserve</a> leaves its key <a href="/wiki/Interest_rate" title="Interest rate">interest rate</a> unchanged at today's meeting, saying that rates will be kept low for a considerable period.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180"><a href="#cite_note-180">[180]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Halloween_solar_storms,_2003" title="Halloween solar storms, 2003">Halloween solar storms, 2003</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Sun" title="Sun">sun</a> emits another <a href="/wiki/Coronal_mass_ejection" title="Coronal mass ejection">coronal mass ejection</a> directly toward the <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">Earth</a>, the third largest <a href="/wiki/Solar_flare" title="Solar flare">solar flare</a> on record. The effects are projected to affect Earth on the 29th.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181"><a href="#cite_note-181">[181]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182"><a href="#cite_note-182">[182]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wildfire" title="Wildfire">Wildfires</a> are largest in California history; 1,500 homes are destroyed, 16 people killed and 600,000 acres (2,400 km<sup>2</sup>) burned. Evacuations are ordered from parts of cities in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_County,_California" title="Los Angeles County, California">Los Angeles</a> and <a href="/wiki/San_Diego_County,_California" title="San Diego County, California">San Diego</a> counties.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183"><a href="#cite_note-183">[183]</a></sup> The conflagration also spreads across the border into the Mexican state of <a href="/wiki/Baja_California" title="Baja California">Baja California</a>, where two deaths are reported.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_(UK)" title="Conservative Party (UK)">The UK Conservative Party</a>'s <a href="/wiki/1922_Committee" title="1922 Committee">1922 Committee</a> announces that leader <a href="/wiki/Iain_Duncan_Smith" title="Iain Duncan Smith">Iain Duncan Smith</a> will face an immediate <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Motion_of_Confidence" title="Motion of Confidence">vote of confidence</a> in his leadership on the following day, after at least 25 <a href="/wiki/Backbencher" title="Backbencher">backbenchers</a> formally request it.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184"><a href="#cite_note-184">[184]</a></sup></li>
<li>The campaign for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Japan_general_election,_2003" title="Japan general election, 2003">Japan general election, 2003</a> starts, lasting until a voting date, Nov 9.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185"><a href="#cite_note-185">[185]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_29.2C_2003_.28Wednesday.29">October 29, 2003 (Wednesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: October 29, 2003 (Wednesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The US <a href="/wiki/Food_and_Drug_Administration" title="Food and Drug Administration">FDA</a> approves Risperdal Consta (<a href="/wiki/Risperidone" title="Risperidone">Risperidone</a> long-acting injection) for the treatment of <a href="/wiki/Schizophrenia" title="Schizophrenia">schizophrenia</a>. Although already approved in several other countries, it is the first long-acting, <a href="/wiki/Atypical_antipsychotic" title="Atypical antipsychotic">atypical antipsychotic</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Medication" title="Medication">medication</a> to be approved by the FDA.</li>
<li>British <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_(UK)" title="Conservative Party (UK)">Conservative Party</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Iain_Duncan_Smith" title="Iain Duncan Smith">Iain Duncan Smith</a> loses a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vote_of_confidence" title="Vote of confidence">vote of confidence</a> in his parliamentary party by 90 votes to 75 and, in accordance with party rules, resigns from the leadership. A new leadership election is called. Shadow Deputy Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Davis_(British_politician)" title="David Davis (British politician)">David Davis</a>, previously tipped as a future leader, surprises Westminster by announcing that he will not seek the leadership and endorses former <a href="/wiki/Home_Secretary" title="Home Secretary">Home Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Michael_Howard" title="Michael Howard">Michael Howard</a>, who is now seen as the frontrunner to assume the leadership. Other leading politicians endorse Howard, once famously described by <a href="/wiki/Ann_Widdecombe" title="Ann Widdecombe">a colleague</a> as having "something of the night about him."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186"><a href="#cite_note-186">[186]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187"><a href="#cite_note-187">[187]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_occupation_of_Iraq" title="American occupation of Iraq">Occupation of Iraq</a>: The International <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Red_Cross" title="Red Cross">Red Cross</a> announces that it is to scale back its commitments to Iraq.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188"><a href="#cite_note-188">[188]</a></sup> Two more GIs are killed, bringing the total killed since May 1 to 115.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189"><a href="#cite_note-189">[189]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Halloween_solar_storms,_2003" title="Halloween solar storms, 2003">Halloween Solar Storms</a>. The Earth's <a href="/wiki/Magnetosphere" title="Magnetosphere">magnetosphere</a> is hit by the recent <a href="/wiki/Solar_flare" title="Solar flare">solar flare</a> causing a brief but intense <a href="/wiki/Geomagnetic_storm" title="Geomagnetic storm">geomagnetic storm</a>, provoking unusual displays of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aurora_(astronomy)" title="Aurora (astronomy)">Northern Lights</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190"><a href="#cite_note-190">[190]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_30.2C_2003_.28Thursday.29">October 30, 2003 (Thursday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: October 30, 2003 (Thursday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>A plastic <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toy_gun" title="Toy gun">toy gun</a>, used as part of a <a href="/wiki/Halloween" title="Halloween">Halloween</a> costume, sparks a two-hour-long <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a> scare at the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Capitol" title="United States Capitol">Capitol</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191"><a href="#cite_note-191">[191]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Commerce" title="United States Department of Commerce">United States Department of Commerce</a> reports that U.S. <a href="/wiki/Gross_domestic_product" title="Gross domestic product">gross domestic product</a> grew at an annual rate of 7.2% in the third quarter, the fastest growth rate since 1984.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192"><a href="#cite_note-192">[192]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> removes his Chief of Staff as the political battle with the "Russian <a href="/wiki/Business_oligarch" title="Business oligarch">oligarchs</a>" and between hard-liners and liberals, continues.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193"><a href="#cite_note-193">[193]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194"><a href="#cite_note-194">[194]</a></sup> Russian judicial authorities have seized control of <a href="/wiki/Yukos" title="Yukos">Yukos</a>, the giant oil company.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195"><a href="#cite_note-195">[195]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraq_War" title="Iraq War">Iraq War</a>: Officials postpone awarding two contracts to repair Iraq's oil refineries and pipelines (primarily because of sabotage and dilapidated conditions).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196"><a href="#cite_note-196">[196]</a></sup> An investigation has been started on the high price that the United States is paying to <a href="/wiki/KBR_(company)" title="KBR (company)">Kellogg Brown &amp; Root</a> for oil imported from <a href="/wiki/Kuwait" title="Kuwait">Kuwait</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197"><a href="#cite_note-197">[197]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Center_for_Public_Integrity" title="Center for Public Integrity">Center for Public Integrity</a> says that firms awarded contracts in Iraq have tended to be big donors (in the past) to the <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198"><a href="#cite_note-198">[198]</a></sup> The UN announces that it is withdrawing its remaining international staff from Baghdad, perhaps temporarily.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199"><a href="#cite_note-199">[199]</a></sup></li>
<li>After 22 years in power, Malaysian Prime Minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mahathir_bin_Mohamad" title="Mahathir bin Mohamad">Mahathir bin Mohamad</a> retires. He is succeeded by Dato' Seri <a href="/wiki/Abdullah_Ahmad_Badawi" title="Abdullah Ahmad Badawi">Abdullah Ahmad Badawi</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200"><a href="#cite_note-200">[200]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October_31.2C_2003_.28Friday.29">October 31, 2003 (Friday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/October_2003&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: October 31, 2003 (Friday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The trial of <a href="/wiki/Shoko_Asahara" title="Shoko Asahara">Shoko Asahara</a>, accused of involvement in the 1995 sarin gas attack on the Tokyo subway, ends in Japan with final statements from lawyers. The next court session is to be held in mid-February 2004.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201"><a href="#cite_note-201">[201]</a></sup></li>
<li>The furor surrounding <a href="/wiki/Yukos" title="Yukos">Yukos</a> deepens with an outspoken statement from the Russian <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister" title="Prime Minister">Prime Minister</a> expressing deep concern about the freezing of Yukos shares.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202"><a href="#cite_note-202">[202]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kenneth_Clarke" title="Kenneth Clarke">Kenneth Clarke</a> has ruled himself out of the contest to lead the UK <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_(UK)" title="Conservative Party (UK)">Conservative Party</a> and the field is left potentially clear for <a href="/wiki/Michael_Howard" title="Michael Howard">Michael Howard</a> to be elected unopposed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203"><a href="#cite_note-203">[203]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
